## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-327">Referencia de plantilla de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-327">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-328">Los tokens entre llaves (`{ ... }`) definen *parámetros de ruta* que se enlazan si se encuentran coincidencias con la ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-328">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-329">Puede definir más de un parámetro de ruta en un segmento de ruta, pero deben estar separados por un valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-329">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-330">Por ejemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` no es una ruta válida, ya que no hay ningún valor literal entre `{controller}` y `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-330">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-331">Estos parámetros de ruta deben tener un nombre y, opcionalmente, atributos adicionales especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-331">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-332">El texto literal diferente de los parámetros de ruta (por ejemplo, `{id}`) y el separador de ruta `/` deben coincidir con el texto de la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-332">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-333">La coincidencia de texto no distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas y se basa en la representación descodificada de la ruta de las direcciones URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-333">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-334">Para que el delimitador de parámetro de ruta literal coincida (`{` o `}`), repita el carácter (`{{` o `}}`) para usarlo como secuencia de escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-334">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-335">Los patrones de dirección URL que intentan capturar un nombre de archivo con una extensión de archivo opcional tienen consideraciones adicionales.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-335">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-336">Por ejemplo, considere la plantilla `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-336">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-337">Cuando existen valores para `filename` y `ext`, los dos valores se rellenan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-337">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-338">Si solo existe un valor para `filename` en la dirección URL, la ruta coincide porque el punto final (`.`) es opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-338">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-339">Las direcciones URL siguientes coinciden con esta ruta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-339">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-340">Se puede usar un asterisco (`*`) o un asterisco doble (`**`) como prefijo de un parámetro de ruta para enlazar con el resto del URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-340">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-341">Se denominan parámetros *comodín*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-341">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-342">Por ejemplo, `blog/{**slug}` coincide con cualquier URI que empiece por `/blog` y que vaya seguido de cualquier valor, que se asigna al valor de ruta `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-342">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-343">Los parámetros comodín también pueden coincidir con una cadena vacía.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-343">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-344">El parámetro catch-all inserta los caracteres de escape correspondientes cuando se usa la ruta para generar una dirección URL, incluidos caracteres de separación de ruta de acceso (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-344">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-345">Por ejemplo, la ruta `foo/{*path}` con valores de ruta `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-345">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-346">Tenga en cuenta la barra diagonal de escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-346">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-347">Para los caracteres separadores de ruta de acceso de ida y vuelta, use el prefijo de parámetro de ruta `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-347">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-348">La ruta `foo/{**path}` con `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-348">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-349">Los parámetros de ruta pueden tener *valores predeterminados* designados mediante la especificación del valor predeterminado después del nombre de parámetro, separado por un signo igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-349">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-350">Por ejemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como el valor predeterminado de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-350">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-351">El valor predeterminado se usa si no hay ningún valor en la dirección URL para el parámetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-351">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-352">Los parámetros de ruta se pueden convertir en opcionales si se anexa un signo de interrogación (`?`) al final del nombre del parámetro, como en `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-352">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-353">La diferencia entre los valores opcionales y los parámetros de ruta predeterminados es que un parámetro de ruta con un valor predeterminado siempre genera un valor, mientras que un parámetro opcional tiene un valor solo cuando la dirección URL de solicitud lo proporciona.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-353">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-354">Los parámetros de ruta pueden tener restricciones que deben coincidir con el valor de ruta enlazado desde la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-354">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-355">Si se agrega un carácter de dos puntos (`:`) y un nombre de restricción después del nombre del parámetro de ruta, se especifica una *restricción insertada* en un parámetro de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-355">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-356">Si la restricción requiere argumentos, se incluyen entre paréntesis (`(...)`) después del nombre de restricción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-356">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-357">Se pueden especificar varias restricciones insertadas si se anexa otro carácter de dos puntos (`:`) y un nombre de restricción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-357">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-358">El nombre de restricción y los argumentos se pasan al servicio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para crear una instancia de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> para su uso en el procesamiento de direcciones URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-358">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-359">Por ejemplo, la plantilla de ruta `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica una restricción `minlength` con el argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-359">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-360">Para obtener más información sobre las restricciones de ruta y una lista de las restricciones proporcionadas por el marco de trabajo, vea la sección [Referencia de restricciones de ruta](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-360">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-361">Los parámetros de ruta también pueden tener transformadores de parámetros, que transforman el valor de un parámetro al generar vínculos y acciones y páginas coincidentes para las direcciones URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-361">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-362">Al igual que las restricciones, los transformadores de parámetros se pueden agregar en línea a un parámetro de ruta al incorporar un carácter de dos puntos (`:`) y un nombre de transformador después del nombre del parámetro de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-362">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-363">Por ejemplo, la plantilla de ruta `blog/{article:slugify}` especifica un transformador `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-363">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-364">Para obtener más información sobre los transformadores de parámetros, vea la sección [Referencia de transformadores de parámetros](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-364">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-365">En la tabla siguiente se muestran algunas plantillas de ruta de ejemplo y su comportamiento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-365">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-366">Plantilla de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-366">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-367">URI coincidente de ejemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-367">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-368">El URI de la solicitud&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-368">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-369">Solo coincide con la ruta de acceso única `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-369">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-370">Coincide y establece `Page` en `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-370">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-371">Coincide y establece `Page` en `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-371">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-372">Se asigna al controlador `Products` y la acción `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-372">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-373">Se asigna al controlador `Products` y la acción `Details` (`id` se establece en 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-373">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-374">Se asigna al controlador `Home` y al método `Index` (`id` se omite).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-374">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-375">El uso de una plantilla suele ser el método de enrutamiento más sencillo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-375">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-376">Las restricciones y los valores predeterminados también se pueden especificar fuera de la plantilla de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-376">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-377">Habilite el [registro](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver de qué forma las implementaciones de enrutamiento integradas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, coinciden con las solicitudes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-377">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-378">Nombres de enrutamientos reservados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-378">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-379">Las siguientes palabras clave son nombres reservados y no se pueden usar como nombres de ruta o parámetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-379">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-380">Referencia de restricción de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-380">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-381">Las restricciones de ruta se ejecutan cuando se ha producido una coincidencia con la dirección URL entrante y la ruta de dirección URL se convierte en tokens en valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-381">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-382">En general, las restricciones de ruta inspeccionan el valor de ruta asociado a través de la plantilla de ruta y deciden si el valor es aceptable o no.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-382">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-383">Algunas restricciones de ruta usan datos ajenos al valor de ruta para decidir si la solicitud se puede enrutar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-383">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-384">Por ejemplo, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> puede aceptar o rechazar una solicitud basada en su verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-384">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-385">Las restricciones se usan en las solicitudes de enrutamiento y la generación de vínculos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-385">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-386">No use las restricciones para las **validación de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-386">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-387">Si las restricciones se usan para la **validación de entrada**, los resultados de entrada no válidos producirán un error *404 - No encontrado* en lugar de un error *400 - Solicitud incorrecta* con un mensaje de error adecuado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-387">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-388">Las restricciones de ruta se usan para **eliminar la ambigüedad** entre rutas similares, no para validar las entradas de una ruta determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-388">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-389">En la tabla siguiente se muestran algunas restricciones de ruta de ejemplo y su comportamiento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-389">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-390">restricción</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-390">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-391">Ejemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-391">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-392">Coincidencias de ejemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-392">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-393">Notas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-393">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-394">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-394">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-395">Coincide con cualquier entero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-395">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-396">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-396">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-397">Coincide con `true` o `false` (no distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-397">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-398">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-398">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-399">Coincide con un valor `DateTime` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-399">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-400">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-400">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-401">Coincide con un valor `decimal` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-401">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-402">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-402">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-403">Coincide con un valor `double` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-403">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-404">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-404">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-405">Coincide con un valor `float` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-405">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-406">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-406">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-407">Coincide con un valor `Guid` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-407">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-408">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-408">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-409">Coincide con un valor `long` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-409">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-410">La cadena debe tener al menos cuatro caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-410">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-411">La cadena no debe tener más de ocho caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-411">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-412">La cadena debe tener una longitud de exactamente 12 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-412">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-413">La cadena debe tener una longitud como mínimo de ocho caracteres y como máximo de 16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-413">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-414">El valor entero debe ser como mínimo 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-414">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-415">El valor entero debe ser como máximo 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-415">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-416">El valor entero debe ser como mínimo 18 y máximo 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-416">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-417">La cadena debe constar de uno o más caracteres alfabéticos (`a`-`z`, no distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-417">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-418">La cadena debe coincidir con la expresión regular (vea las sugerencias sobre cómo definir una expresión regular)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-418">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-419">Se usa para exigir que un valor que no es de parámetro esté presente durante la generación de dirección URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-419">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-420">Es posible aplicar varias restricciones delimitadas por dos puntos a un único parámetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-420">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-421">Por ejemplo, la siguiente restricción permite limitar un parámetro a un valor entero de 1 o superior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-421">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-422">Las restricciones de ruta que comprueban la dirección URL y que se convierten en un tipo CLR (como `int` o `DateTime`) usan siempre la referencia cultural invariable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-422">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-423">Estas restricciones dan por supuesto que la dirección URL no es localizable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-423">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-424">Las restricciones de ruta proporcionadas por el marco de trabajo no modifican los valores almacenados en los valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-424">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-425">Todos los valores de ruta analizados desde la dirección URL se almacenan como cadenas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-425">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-426">Por ejemplo, la restricción `float` intenta convertir el valor de ruta en un valor Float, pero el valor convertido se usa exclusivamente para comprobar que se puede convertir en Float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-426">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-427">Expresiones regulares</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-427">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-428">El marco de trabajo de ASP.NET Core agrega `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` al constructor de expresiones regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-428">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-429">Vea <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obtener una descripción de estos miembros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-429">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-430">Las expresiones regulares usan delimitadores y tokens similares a los que usan el enrutamiento y el lenguaje C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-430">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-431">Es necesario usar secuencias de escape con los tokens de expresiones regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-431">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-432">Para usar la expresión regular `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` en el enrutamiento, los caracteres `\` (una barra diagonal inversa) de la cadena se deben proporcionar como caracteres `\\` (barra diagonal inversa doble) en el archivo de código fuente de C# para que el carácter de escape de cadena `\` tenga una secuencia de escape (a menos que se usen [literales de cadena textuales](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-432">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-433">Para aplicar secuencias de escape a los caracteres delimitadores de parámetro de enrutamiento (`{`, `}`, `[` y `]`), duplique los caracteres en la expresión (`{{`, `}`, `[[` y `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-433">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-434">En la tabla siguiente se muestra una expresión regular y la versión con la secuencia de escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-434">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-435">Expresión regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-435">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-436">Expresión regular con secuencia de escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-436">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-437">Las expresiones regulares que se usan en el enrutamiento suelen empezar con el carácter de acento circunflejo (`^`) y coinciden con la posición inicial de la cadena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-437">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-438">Las expresiones suelen terminar con el carácter del signo de dólar (`$`) y coincidir con el final de la cadena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-438">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-439">Los caracteres `^` y `$` garantizan que la expresión regular coincide con el valor completo del parámetro de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-439">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-440">Sin los caracteres `^` y `$`, la expresión regular coincide con cualquier subcadena de la cadena, algo que normalmente no es deseable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-440">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-441">En la tabla siguiente se proporcionan ejemplos y se explica por qué coinciden o no.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-441">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-442">Expresión</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-442">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-443">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-443">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-444">Coincidir con</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-444">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-445">Comentario</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-445">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-446">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-446">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-447">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-447">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-448">Coincidencias de subcadenas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-448">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-449">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-449">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-450">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-450">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-451">Coincidencias de subcadenas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-451">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-452">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-452">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-453">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-453">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-454">Coincide con la expresión</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-454">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-455">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-455">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-456">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-456">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-457">No distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-457">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-458">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-458">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-459">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-459">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-460">Vea `^` y `$` más arriba</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-460">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-461">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-461">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-462">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-462">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-463">Vea `^` y `$` más arriba</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-463">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-464">Para obtener más información sobre la sintaxis de expresiones regulares, vea [Expresiones regulares de .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-464">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-465">Para restringir un parámetro a un conjunto conocido de valores posibles, use una expresión regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-465">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-466">Por ejemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` solo hace coincidir el valor de ruta `action` con `list`, `get` o `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-466">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-467">Si se pasa al diccionario de restricciones, la cadena `^(list|get|create)$` es equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-467">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-468">Las restricciones que se pasan al diccionario de restricciones (no insertado en una plantilla) que no coinciden con una de las restricciones conocidas también se tratan como expresiones regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-468">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-469">Restricciones de ruta personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-469">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-470">Además de las restricciones de ruta integradas, se pueden crear restricciones de ruta personalizadas implementando la interfaz <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-470">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-471">La interfaz <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contiene un único método, `Match`, que devuelve `true` si se cumple la restricción, y `false` en caso contrario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-471">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-472">Para utilizar una restricción <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizada, el tipo de restricción de ruta debe registrarse con el parámetro <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> de la aplicación en el contenedor de servicios de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-472">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-473"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> es un diccionario que asigna claves de restricciones de ruta a implementaciones de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> que validen esas restricciones.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-473">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-474">El parámetro <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> de una aplicación puede actualizarse en `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de una llamada a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) o configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directamente con `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-474">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-475">Por ejemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-475">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-476">La restricción puede aplicarse a las rutas de la manera habitual, usando el nombre especificado al registrar el tipo de restricción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-476">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-477">Por ejemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-477">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-478">Referencia de transformadores de parámetros</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-478">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-479">Transformadores de parámetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-479">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-480">Se ejecutan al generar un vínculo para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-480">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-481">Implemente `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-481">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-482">Se configuran con <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-482">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-483">Toman el valor de ruta del parámetro y lo transforman en un nuevo valor de cadena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-483">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-484">Como resultado, el valor transformado se usa en el vínculo generado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-484">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-485">Por ejemplo, un transformador de parámetros personalizado `slugify` en el patrón de ruta `blog\{article:slugify}` con `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` genera `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-485">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-486">Para usar un transformador de parámetros en un patrón de ruta, configúrelo primero con <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> en `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-486">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-487">El marco usa los transformadores de parámetros para transformar el URI en el que se resuelve un punto de conexión.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-487">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-488">Por ejemplo, ASP.NET Core MVC usa transformadores de parámetros para transformar el valor de ruta usado para hacer coincidir elementos `area`, `controller`, `action` y `page`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-488">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-489">Con la ruta anterior, la acción `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` coincide con el URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-489">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll()` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-490">Un transformador de parámetros no cambia los valores de ruta usados para generar un vínculo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-490">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-491">Por ejemplo, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` genera `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-491">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-492">ASP.NET Core proporciona las convenciones de API para usar transformadores de parámetros con rutas generadas:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-492">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-493">ASP.NET Core MVC tiene la convención de API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-493">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-494">Esta convención aplica un transformador de parámetro especificado a todas las rutas de atributo de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-494">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-495">El transformador de parámetro transforma los tokens de rutas de atributo a medida que se reemplazan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-495">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-496">Para más información, consulte [Usar un transformador de parámetro para personalizar el reemplazo de tokens](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-496">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-497">Razor Pages tiene la convención de API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-497">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-498">Esta convención aplica un transformador de parámetros especificado a todas las instancias de Razor Pages detectadas de forma automática.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-498">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-499">El transformador de parámetros transforma los segmentos de nombre de archivo y carpeta de las rutas de Razor Pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-499">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-500">Para más información, consulte el artículo sobre cómo [usar un transformador de parámetro para personalizar rutas de Razor Pages](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-500">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-501">Referencia de generación de direcciones URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-501">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-502">En el ejemplo siguiente se muestra cómo se genera un vínculo a una ruta, dado un diccionario de valores de ruta y un valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-502">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-503">El valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generado al final del ejemplo anterior es `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-503">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-504">El diccionario proporciona los valores de ruta `operation` e `id` de la plantilla "Ruta de paquete de seguimiento", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-504">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-505">Para obtener más información, vea el código de ejemplo de la sección [Uso de software intermedio de enrutamiento](#use-routing-middleware) o la [aplicación de ejemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-505">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-506">El segundo parámetro del constructor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> es una colección de *valores de ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-506">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-507">Los valores de ambiente son adecuados porque limitan el número de valores que el desarrollador debe especificar dentro de un contexto de solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-507">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-508">Los valores de ruta actuales de la solicitud actual se consideran valores de ambiente para la generación de vínculos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-508">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-509">En la acción `About` de `HomeController` de una aplicación ASP.NET Core MVC, no es necesario especificar el valor de ruta de controlador para vincular a la acción `Index` (se usará el valor de ambiente `Home`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-509">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-510">Los valores de ambiente que no coincidan con un parámetro se omiten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-510">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-511">También se omiten los valores de ambiente cuando un valor proporcionado de forma explícita invalida el valor de ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-511">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-512">La coincidencia se produce de izquierda a derecha en la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-512">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-513">Los valores que se proporcionan de forma explícita pero que no coinciden con un segmento de la ruta se agregan a la cadena de consulta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-513">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-514">En la tabla siguiente se muestra el resultado cuando se usa la plantilla de ruta `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-514">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-515">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-515">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-516">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-516">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-517">Resultado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-517">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-518">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-518">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-519">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-519">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-520">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-520">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-521">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-521">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-522">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-522">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-523">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-523">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-524">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-524">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-525">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-525">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-526">Si una ruta tiene un valor predeterminado que no se corresponde con un parámetro y ese valor se proporciona de forma explícita, debe coincidir con el valor predeterminado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-526">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-527">La generación de vínculos solo genera un vínculo para esta ruta si se proporcionan los valores coincidentes para `controller` y `action`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-527">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-528">Segmentos complejos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-528">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-529">Los segmentos complejos (por ejemplo, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`), se procesan buscando coincidencias de literales de derecha a izquierda de un modo no expansivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-529">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-530">Consulte [este código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) para obtener una explicación detallada de cómo se comparan los segmentos complejos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-530">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-531">El [código de ejemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) no se usa en ASP.NET Core, pero proporciona una buena explicación de los segmentos complejos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-531">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
