<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1002">Las solicitudes entrantes especifican la clase <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>, que llama al método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> en cada ruta de la secuencia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1002">Incoming requests enter the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RouterMiddleware>, which calls the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> method on each route in sequence.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1003">La instancia de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> decide si *controla* la solicitud mediante el establecimiento de [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler*) en un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> que no sea NULL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1003">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> instance chooses whether to *handle* the request by setting the [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler*) to a non-null <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1004">Si una ruta establece un controlador para la solicitud, el procesamiento de rutas se detiene y se invoca el controlador para procesar la solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1004">If a route sets a handler for the request, route processing stops, and the handler is invoked to process the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1005">Si no se encuentra ningún controlador de ruta para procesar la solicitud, el middleware entrega la solicitud al siguiente middleware en la canalización de solicitudes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1005">If no route handler is found to process the request, the middleware hands the request off to the next middleware in the request pipeline.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1006">La entrada principal para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> es el [RouteContext.HttpContext](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.HttpContext*) asociado a la solicitud actual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1006">The primary input to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is the [RouteContext.HttpContext](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.HttpContext*) associated with the current request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1007">[RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler) y [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData*) son salidas que se establecen después de que una ruta coincida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1007">The [RouteContext.Handler](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.Handler) and [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData*) are outputs set after a route is matched.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1008">Una coincidencia que llama a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> también establece las propiedades de [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) en los valores adecuados en función del procesamiento de solicitudes realizado hasta el momento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1008">A match that calls <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> also sets the properties of the [RouteContext.RouteData](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteContext.RouteData) to appropriate values based on the request processing performed thus far.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1009">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) es un diccionario de los *valores de ruta* generados desde la ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1009">[RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values*) is a dictionary of *route values* produced from the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1010">Estos valores se suelen determinar mediante la conversión en tokens de la dirección URL, y se pueden usar para aceptar la entrada del usuario o para tomar otras decisiones sobre el envío dentro de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1010">These values are usually determined by tokenizing the URL and can be used to accept user input or to make further dispatching decisions inside the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1011">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) es un contenedor de propiedades de datos adicionales relacionados con la ruta coincidente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1011">[RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) is a property bag of additional data related to the matched route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1012">Se proporcionan <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> para permitir la asociación de datos de estado con cada ruta, de modo que la aplicación pueda tomar decisiones en función de las rutas que han coincidido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1012"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*> are provided to support associating state data with each route so that the app can make decisions based on which route matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1013">Estos valores los define el desarrollador y **no** afectan de ninguna manera al comportamiento del enrutamiento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1013">These values are developer-defined and do **not** affect the behavior of routing in any way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1014">Además, los valores que se guardan provisionalmente en [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) pueden ser de cualquier tipo, a diferencia de [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), que deben poder convertirse fácilmente en cadenas y a partir de estas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1014">Additionally, values stashed in [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*) can be of any type, in contrast to [RouteData.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Values), which must be convertible to and from strings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1015">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) es una lista de las rutas que han participado en encontrar una coincidencia correcta con la solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1015">[RouteData.Routers](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers) is a list of the routes that took part in successfully matching the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1016">Las rutas se pueden anidar unas dentro de otras.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1016">Routes can be nested inside of one another.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1017">La propiedad <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> refleja la ruta de acceso del árbol lógico de rutas que han tenido como resultado una coincidencia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1017">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> property reflects the path through the logical tree of routes that resulted in a match.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1018">Por lo general, el primer elemento de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> es la colección de rutas y se debe usar para la generación de direcciones URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1018">Generally, the first item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route collection and should be used for URL generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1019">El último elemento de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> es el controlador de ruta que ha coincidido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1019">The last item in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.Routers> is the route handler that matched.</span></span>

<a name="lg"></a>

### <a name="url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1020">Generación de dirección URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1020">URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1021">La generación de dirección URL es el proceso por el cual el enrutamiento puede crear una ruta de dirección URL basada en un conjunto de valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1021">URL generation is the process by which routing can create a URL path based on a set of route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1022">Esto permite una separación lógica entre los controladores de ruta y las direcciones URL que tienen acceso a ellos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1022">This allows for a logical separation between route handlers and the URLs that access them.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1023">La generación de direcciones URL sigue un proceso iterativo similar, pero se inicia cuando el código de usuario o de marco de trabajo llama al método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> de la colección de rutas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1023">URL generation follows a similar iterative process, but it starts with user or framework code calling into the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> method of the route collection.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1024">Se llama en secuencia al método <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> de cada *ruta* hasta que se devuelva un valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> distinto de NULL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1024">Each *route* has its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> method called in sequence until a non-null <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> is returned.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1025">La principal entradas de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> son:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1025">The primary inputs to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> are:</span></span>

* [<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1026">VirtualPathContext.HttpContext</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1026">VirtualPathContext.HttpContext</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext)
* [<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1027">VirtualPathContext.Values</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1027">VirtualPathContext.Values</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values)
* [<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1028">VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1028">VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues)

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1029">Las rutas usan principalmente los valores de ruta proporcionados por <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> y <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> para decidir si es posible generar una dirección URL y qué valores se van a incluir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1029">Routes primarily use the route values provided by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> to decide whether it's possible to generate a URL and what values to include.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1030"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> son el conjunto de valores de ruta producidos a partir de la coincidencia con la solicitud actual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1030">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues> are the set of route values that were produced from matching the current request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1031">En cambio, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> son los valores de ruta que especifican cómo se genera la dirección URL deseada para la operación actual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1031">In contrast, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values> are the route values that specify how to generate the desired URL for the current operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1032">Se proporciona <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext> por si una ruta debe obtener servicios o datos adicionales asociados con el contexto actual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1032">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.HttpContext> is provided in case a route should obtain services or additional data associated with the current context.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1033">Piense en [VirtualPathContext.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values*) como un conjunto de invalidaciones para [VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1033">Think of [VirtualPathContext.Values](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.Values*) as a set of overrides for the [VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext.AmbientValues*).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1034">La generación de direcciones URL intenta reutilizar los valores de ruta de la solicitud actual para generar direcciones URL para los vínculos con la misma ruta o valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1034">URL generation attempts to reuse route values from the current request to generate URLs for links using the same route or route values.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1035">La salida de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> es <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1035">The output of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1036"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> es un valor paralelo de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1036"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> is a parallel of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1037"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> contiene el valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> de la dirección URL de salida y algunas propiedades más que la ruta debe establecer.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1037"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData> contains the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> for the output URL and some additional properties that should be set by the route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1038">La propiedad [VirtualPathData.VirtualPath](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath*) contiene la *ruta de acceso virtual* generada por la ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1038">The [VirtualPathData.VirtualPath](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath*) property contains the *virtual path* produced by the route.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1039">Es posible que deba procesar aún más la ruta de acceso, según sus necesidades.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1039">Depending on your needs, you may need to process the path further.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1040">Si quiere representar la dirección URL generada en HTML, anteponga la ruta de acceso base de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1040">If you want to render the generated URL in HTML, prepend the base path of the app.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1041">[VirtualPathData.Router](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.Router*) es una referencia a la ruta que ha generado correctamente la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1041">The [VirtualPathData.Router](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.Router*) is a reference to the route that successfully generated the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1042">La propiedad [VirtualPathData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.DataTokens*) es un diccionario de datos adicionales relacionados con la ruta que ha generado la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1042">The [VirtualPathData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.DataTokens*) properties is a dictionary of additional data related to the route that generated the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1043">Se trata del valor paralelo de [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1043">This is the parallel of [RouteData.DataTokens](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteData.DataTokens*).</span></span>

### <a name="create-routes"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1044">Creación de rutas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1044">Create routes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1045">El enrutamiento proporciona la clase <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> como implementación estándar de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1045">Routing provides the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class as the standard implementation of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1046"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> usa la sintaxis de *plantilla de ruta* para definir patrones que se hacen coincidir con la ruta de dirección URL cuando se llama a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1046"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the *route template* syntax to define patterns to match against the URL path when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.RouteAsync*> is called.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1047"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> usa la misma plantilla de ruta para generar una dirección URL cuando se llama a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1047"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> uses the same route template to generate a URL when <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter.GetVirtualPath*> is called.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1048">La mayoría de las aplicaciones crea rutas mediante una llamada a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> o a uno de los métodos de extensión similares definidos en <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1048">Most apps create routes by calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> or one of the similar extension methods defined on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1049">Todos los métodos de extensión <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> crean una instancia de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> y la agregan a la colección de rutas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1049">Any of the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteBuilder> extension methods create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> and add it to the route collection.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1050"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> no acepta un parámetro de controlador de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1050"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> doesn't accept a route handler parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1051"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> solo agrega las rutas que se controlan mediante <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1051"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> only adds routes that are handled by the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1052">El controlador predeterminado es un elemento `IRouter`, y es posible que el controlador no pueda atender la solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1052">The default handler is an `IRouter`, and the handler might not handle the request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1053">Por ejemplo, ASP.NET Core MVC se suele configurar como un controlador predeterminado que solo controla las solicitudes que coinciden con un controlador y una acción disponibles.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1053">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC is typically configured as a default handler that only handles requests that match an available controller and action.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1054">Para obtener más información sobre el enrutamiento en MVC, vea <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1054">To learn more about routing in MVC, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1055">El código siguiente es un ejemplo de una llamada a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> usada por una definición de ruta típica de ASP.NET Core MVC:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1055">The following code example is an example of a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> call used by a typical ASP.NET Core MVC route definition:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1056">Esta plantilla coincide con una ruta de dirección URL y extrae los valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1056">This template matches a URL path and extracts the route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1057">Por ejemplo, la ruta de acceso `/Products/Details/17` genera los valores de ruta siguientes: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1057">For example, the path `/Products/Details/17` generates the following route values: `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 17 }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1058">Los valores de ruta se determinan al dividir la ruta de dirección URL en segmentos y hacer coincidir cada segmento con el nombre del *parámetro de ruta* en la plantilla de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1058">Route values are determined by splitting the URL path into segments and matching each segment with the *route parameter* name in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1059">Los parámetros de ruta tienen un nombre asignado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1059">Route parameters are named.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1060">Para definir los parámetros, el nombre del parámetro se incluye entre llaves `{ ... }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1060">The parameters defined by enclosing the parameter name in braces `{ ... }`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1061">La plantilla anterior también podría coincidir con la ruta de dirección URL `/` y generar los valores `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1061">The preceding template could also match the URL path `/` and produce the values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1062">Esto se debe a que los parámetros de ruta `{controller}` y `{action}` tienen valores predeterminados y el parámetro de ruta `id` es opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1062">This occurs because the `{controller}` and `{action}` route parameters have default values and the `id` route parameter is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1063">Un signo igual (`=`) seguido de un valor después del nombre del parámetro de ruta define un valor predeterminado para el parámetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1063">An equals sign (`=`) followed by a value after the route parameter name defines a default value for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1064">Un signo de interrogación (`?`) después del nombre del parámetro de ruta define un parámetro opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1064">A question mark (`?`) after the route parameter name defines an optional parameter.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1065">Los parámetros de ruta con un valor predeterminado *siempre* generan un valor de ruta cuando la ruta coincide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1065">Route parameters with a default value *always* produce a route value when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1066">Los parámetros opcionales no generan un valor de ruta si no existió el segmento de ruta de dirección URL correspondiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1066">Optional parameters don't produce a route value if there was no corresponding URL path segment.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1067">Vea la sección [Referencia de plantilla de ruta](#route-template-reference) para obtener una descripción detallada de los escenarios y la sintaxis de la plantilla de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1067">See the [Route template reference](#route-template-reference) section for a thorough description of route template scenarios and syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1068">En el ejemplo siguiente, la definición de parámetro de ruta `{id:int}` define una [restricción de ruta](#route-constraint-reference) para el parámetro de ruta `id`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1068">In the following example, the route parameter definition `{id:int}` defines a [route constraint](#route-constraint-reference) for the `id` route parameter:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id:int}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1069">Esta plantilla coincide con una ruta de dirección URL como `/Products/Details/17`, pero no con `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1069">This template matches a URL path like `/Products/Details/17` but not `/Products/Details/Apples`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1070">Las restricciones de ruta implementan <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> e inspeccionan los valores de ruta para comprobarlos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1070">Route constraints implement <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> and inspect route values to verify them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1071">En este ejemplo, el valor de ruta `id` debe poder convertirse en un entero.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1071">In this example, the route value `id` must be convertible to an integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1072">Vea la [Referencia de restricción de ruta](#route-constraint-reference) para obtener una explicación de las restricciones de ruta proporcionadas por el marco de trabajo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1072">See [route-constraint-reference](#route-constraint-reference) for an explanation of route constraints provided by the framework.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1073">Las sobrecargas adicionales de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> aceptan valores para `constraints`, `dataTokens` y `defaults`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1073">Additional overloads of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> accept values for `constraints`, `dataTokens`, and `defaults`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1074">Estos parámetros suelen usarse para pasar un objeto de tipo anónimo, donde los nombres de propiedad del tipo anónimo coinciden con los nombres de los parámetros de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1074">The typical usage of these parameters is to pass an anonymously typed object, where the property names of the anonymous type match route parameter names.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1075">En los ejemplos <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> siguientes se crean rutas equivalentes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1075">The following <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapRouteRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*> examples create equivalent routes:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller}/{action}/{id?}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Home", action = "Index" });

routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default_route",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1076">La sintaxis insertada para definir las restricciones y los valores predeterminados puede ser conveniente para las rutas simples.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1076">The inline syntax for defining constraints and defaults can be convenient for simple routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1077">Pero hay algunos escenarios, como los tokens de datos, que no son compatibles con la sintaxis insertada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1077">However, there are scenarios, such as data tokens, that aren't supported by inline syntax.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1078">En el ejemplo siguiente se muestran algunos escenarios más:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1078">The following example demonstrates a few additional scenarios:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "blog",
    template: "Blog/{*article}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadArticle" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1079">La plantilla anterior coincide con una ruta de dirección URL como `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` y extrae los valores `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1079">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/Blog/All-About-Routing/Introduction` and extracts the values `{ controller = Blog, action = ReadArticle, article = All-About-Routing/Introduction }`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1080">La ruta genera los valores de ruta predeterminados para `controller` y `action`, incluso si no hay parámetros de ruta correspondientes en la plantilla.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1080">The default route values for `controller` and `action` are produced by the route even though there are no corresponding route parameters in the template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1081">Los valores predeterminados pueden especificarse en la plantilla de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1081">Default values can be specified in the route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1082">El parámetro de ruta `article` se define como un *comodín* por la aparición de un asterisco (`*`) antes del nombre del parámetro de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1082">The `article` route parameter is defined as a *catch-all* by the appearance of an asterisk (`*`) before the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1083">Los parámetros de ruta comodín capturan el resto de la ruta de dirección URL y también pueden coincidir con la cadena vacía.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1083">Catch-all route parameters capture the remainder of the URL path and can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1084">En el ejemplo siguiente se agregan restricciones de ruta y tokens de datos:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1084">The following example adds route constraints and data tokens:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "us_english_products",
    template: "en-US/Products/{id}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Products", action = "Details" },
    constraints: new { id = new IntRouteConstraint() },
    dataTokens: new { locale = "en-US" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1085">La plantilla anterior coincide con una ruta de dirección URL como `/en-US/Products/5` y extrae los valores `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` y los tokens de datos `{ locale = en-US }`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1085">The preceding template matches a URL path like `/en-US/Products/5` and extracts the values `{ controller = Products, action = Details, id = 5 }` and the data tokens `{ locale = en-US }`.</span></span>

![Tokens de Windows de variables locales](routing/_static/tokens.png)

### <a name="route-class-url-generation"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1087">Generación de direcciones URL de clase de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1087">Route class URL generation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1088">La clase <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> también puede llevar a cabo la generación de dirección URL mediante la combinación de un conjunto de valores de ruta con su plantilla de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1088">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class can also perform URL generation by combining a set of route values with its route template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1089">Se trata lógicamente del proceso inverso de hacer coincidir la ruta de dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1089">This is logically the reverse process of matching the URL path.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1090">Para entender mejor la generación de direcciones URL, imagine qué dirección URL quiere generar y, después, piense cómo coincidiría una plantilla de ruta con esa dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1090">To better understand URL generation, imagine what URL you want to generate and then think about how a route template would match that URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1091">¿Qué valores se generarían?</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1091">What values would be produced?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1092">Este es un equivalente aproximado de cómo funciona la generación de dirección URL en la clase <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1092">This is the rough equivalent of how URL generation works in the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route> class.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1093">En el ejemplo siguiente se usa una ruta predeterminada de ASP.NET Core MVC general:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1093">The following example uses a general ASP.NET Core MVC default route:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1094">Con los valores de ruta `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, se genera la dirección URL `/Products/List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1094">With the route values `{ controller = Products, action = List }`, the URL `/Products/List` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1095">Los valores de ruta se sustituyen por los parámetros de ruta correspondientes para formar la ruta de dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1095">The route values are substituted for the corresponding route parameters to form the URL path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1096">Como `id` es un parámetro de ruta opcional, la dirección URL se ha generado correctamente sin ningún valor para `id`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1096">Since `id` is an optional route parameter, the URL is successfully generated without a value for `id`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1097">Con los valores de ruta `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, se genera la dirección URL `/`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1097">With the route values `{ controller = Home, action = Index }`, the URL `/` is generated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1098">Los valores de ruta proporcionados coinciden con los valores predeterminados, y los segmentos correspondientes a los valores predeterminados se omiten sin ningún riesgo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1098">The provided route values match the default values, and the segments corresponding to the default values are safely omitted.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1099">Ambas direcciones URL generadas realizan un recorrido de ida y vuelta con la definición de ruta siguiente (`/Home/Index` y `/`) y generan los mismos valores de ruta que se usaron para generar la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1099">Both URLs generated round-trip with the following route definition (`/Home/Index` and `/`) produce the same route values that were used to generate the URL.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1100">Las aplicaciones con ASP.NET Core MVC deben usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> para generar direcciones URL en lugar de llamar directamente al enrutamiento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1100">An app using ASP.NET Core MVC should use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.Routing.UrlHelper> to generate URLs instead of calling into routing directly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1101">Para obtener más información sobre la generación de direcciones URL, vea la sección [Referencia de generación de direcciones URL](#url-generation-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1101">For more information on URL generation, see the [Url generation reference](#url-generation-reference) section.</span></span>

## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1102">Uso de software intermedio de enrutamiento</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1102">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1103">Haga referencia al [metapaquete Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) en el archivo de proyecto de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1103">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1104">Agregue enrutamiento al contenedor de servicios en `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1104">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1105">Las rutas se deben configurar en el método `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1105">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1106">En la aplicación de ejemplo se usan las API siguientes:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1106">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1107"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; solo coincide con solicitudes HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1107"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> &ndash; Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1108">En la tabla siguiente se muestran las respuestas con los URI especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1108">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1109">Identificador URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1109">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1110">Respuesta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1110">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1111">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1111">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1112">Valores de ruta: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1112">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1113">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1113">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1114">Valores de ruta: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1114">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1115">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1115">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1116">Valores de ruta: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1116">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1117">La solicitud pasa; no hay ninguna coincidencia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1117">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1118">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1118">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1119">La solicitud pasa; solo coincide con HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1119">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1120">La solicitud pasa; no hay ninguna coincidencia.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1120">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1121">Si va a configurar una única ruta, pase una instancia de `IRouter` para llamar a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1121">If you're configuring a single route, call <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*> passing in an `IRouter` instance.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1122">No tendrá que usar <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1122">You won't need to use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1123">El marco de trabajo proporciona un conjunto de métodos de extensión para crear rutas (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1123">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1124">Algunos de los métodos enumerados, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, requieren un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1124">Some of listed methods, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, require a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1125">El valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> se usa como *controlador de ruta* cuando la ruta coincida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1125">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> is used as the *route handler* when the route matches.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1126">Otros métodos de esta familia permiten configurar una canalización de software intermedio para usarla como controlador de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1126">Other methods in this family allow configuring a middleware pipeline for use as the route handler.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1127">Si el método `Map*` no acepta un controlador, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, usa <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1127">If the `Map*` method doesn't accept a handler, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>, it uses the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder.DefaultHandler*>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1128">Los métodos `Map[Verb]` usan restricciones para limitar la ruta al verbo HTTP en el nombre del método.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1128">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1129">Por ejemplo, vea <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> y <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1129">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1130">Referencia de plantilla de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1130">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1131">Los tokens entre llaves (`{ ... }`) definen *parámetros de ruta* que se enlazan si se encuentran coincidencias con la ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1131">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1132">Puede definir más de un parámetro de ruta en un segmento de ruta, pero deben estar separados por un valor literal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1132">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1133">Por ejemplo, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` no es una ruta válida, ya que no hay ningún valor literal entre `{controller}` y `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1133">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1134">Estos parámetros de ruta deben tener un nombre y, opcionalmente, atributos adicionales especificados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1134">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1135">El texto literal diferente de los parámetros de ruta (por ejemplo, `{id}`) y el separador de ruta `/` deben coincidir con el texto de la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1135">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1136">La coincidencia de texto no distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas y se basa en la representación descodificada de la ruta de las direcciones URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1136">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1137">Para que el delimitador de parámetro de ruta literal coincida (`{` o `}`), repita el carácter (`{{` o `}}`) para usarlo como secuencia de escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1137">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1138">Los patrones de dirección URL que intentan capturar un nombre de archivo con una extensión de archivo opcional tienen consideraciones adicionales.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1138">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1139">Por ejemplo, considere la plantilla `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1139">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1140">Cuando existen valores para `filename` y `ext`, los dos valores se rellenan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1140">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1141">Si solo existe un valor para `filename` en la dirección URL, la ruta coincide porque el punto final (`.`) es opcional.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1141">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1142">Las direcciones URL siguientes coinciden con esta ruta:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1142">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1143">Se puede usar el asterisco (`*`) como prefijo de un parámetro de ruta para enlazar con el resto del URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1143">You can use the asterisk (`*`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1144">Es lo que se denomina un parámetro *comodín*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1144">This is called a *catch-all* parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1145">Por ejemplo, `blog/{*slug}` coincide con cualquier URI que empiece por `/blog` y que vaya seguido de cualquier valor, que se asigna al valor de ruta `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1145">For example, `blog/{*slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1146">Los parámetros comodín también pueden coincidir con una cadena vacía.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1146">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1147">El parámetro catch-all inserta los caracteres de escape correspondientes cuando se usa la ruta para generar una dirección URL, incluidos caracteres de separación de ruta de acceso (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1147">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1148">Por ejemplo, la ruta `foo/{*path}` con valores de ruta `{ path = "my/path" }` genera `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1148">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1149">Tenga en cuenta la barra diagonal de escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1149">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1150">Los parámetros de ruta pueden tener *valores predeterminados* designados mediante la especificación del valor predeterminado después del nombre de parámetro, separado por un signo igual (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1150">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1151">Por ejemplo, `{controller=Home}` define `Home` como el valor predeterminado de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1151">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1152">El valor predeterminado se usa si no hay ningún valor en la dirección URL para el parámetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1152">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1153">Los parámetros de ruta se pueden convertir en opcionales si se anexa un signo de interrogación (`?`) al final del nombre del parámetro, como en `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1153">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1154">La diferencia entre los valores opcionales y los parámetros de ruta predeterminados es que un parámetro de ruta con un valor predeterminado siempre genera un valor, mientras que un parámetro opcional tiene un valor solo cuando la dirección URL de solicitud lo proporciona.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1154">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1155">Los parámetros de ruta pueden tener restricciones que deben coincidir con el valor de ruta enlazado desde la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1155">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1156">Si se agrega un carácter de dos puntos (`:`) y un nombre de restricción después del nombre del parámetro de ruta, se especifica una *restricción insertada* en un parámetro de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1156">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1157">Si la restricción requiere argumentos, se incluyen entre paréntesis (`(...)`) después del nombre de restricción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1157">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1158">Se pueden especificar varias restricciones insertadas si se anexa otro carácter de dos puntos (`:`) y un nombre de restricción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1158">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1159">El nombre de restricción y los argumentos se pasan al servicio <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> para crear una instancia de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> para su uso en el procesamiento de direcciones URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1159">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1160">Por ejemplo, la plantilla de ruta `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` especifica una restricción `minlength` con el argumento `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1160">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1161">Para obtener más información sobre las restricciones de ruta y una lista de las restricciones proporcionadas por el marco de trabajo, vea la sección [Referencia de restricciones de ruta](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1161">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1162">En la tabla siguiente se muestran algunas plantillas de ruta de ejemplo y su comportamiento.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1162">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1163">Plantilla de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1163">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1164">URI coincidente de ejemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1164">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1165">El URI de la solicitud&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1165">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1166">Solo coincide con la ruta de acceso única `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1166">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1167">Coincide y establece `Page` en `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1167">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1168">Coincide y establece `Page` en `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1168">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1169">Se asigna al controlador `Products` y la acción `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1169">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1170">Se asigna al controlador `Products` y la acción `Details` (`id` se establece en 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1170">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1171">Se asigna al controlador `Home` y al método `Index` (`id` se omite).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1171">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1172">El uso de una plantilla suele ser el método de enrutamiento más sencillo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1172">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1173">Las restricciones y los valores predeterminados también se pueden especificar fuera de la plantilla de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1173">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1174">Habilite el [registro](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) para ver de qué forma las implementaciones de enrutamiento integradas, como <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, coinciden con las solicitudes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1174">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1175">Nombres de enrutamientos reservados</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1175">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1176">Las siguientes palabras clave son nombres reservados y no se pueden usar como nombres de ruta o parámetros:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1176">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1177">Referencia de restricción de ruta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1177">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1178">Las restricciones de ruta se ejecutan cuando se ha producido una coincidencia con la dirección URL entrante y la ruta de dirección URL se convierte en tokens en valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1178">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1179">En general, las restricciones de ruta inspeccionan el valor de ruta asociado a través de la plantilla de ruta y deciden si el valor es aceptable o no.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1179">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1180">Algunas restricciones de ruta usan datos ajenos al valor de ruta para decidir si la solicitud se puede enrutar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1180">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1181">Por ejemplo, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> puede aceptar o rechazar una solicitud basada en su verbo HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1181">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1182">Las restricciones se usan en las solicitudes de enrutamiento y la generación de vínculos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1182">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1183">No use las restricciones para las **validación de entrada**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1183">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1184">Si las restricciones se usan para la **validación de entrada**, los resultados de entrada no válidos producirán un error *404 - No encontrado* en lugar de un error *400 - Solicitud incorrecta* con un mensaje de error adecuado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1184">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1185">Las restricciones de ruta se usan para **eliminar la ambigüedad** entre rutas similares, no para validar las entradas de una ruta determinada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1185">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1186">En la tabla siguiente se muestran algunas restricciones de ruta de ejemplo y su comportamiento esperado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1186">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1187">restricción</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1187">constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1188">Ejemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1188">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1189">Coincidencias de ejemplo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1189">Example Matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1190">Notas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1190">Notes</span></span> |
| ---------- | ------- | --------------- | ----- |
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1191">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1191">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1192">Coincide con cualquier entero</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1192">Matches any integer</span></span> |
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1193">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1193">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1194">Coincide con `true` o `false` (no distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1194">Matches `true` or `false` (case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1195">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1195">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1196">Coincide con un valor `DateTime` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1196">Matches a valid `DateTime` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1197">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1197">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1198">Coincide con un valor `decimal` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1198">Matches a valid `decimal` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1199">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1199">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1200">Coincide con un valor `double` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1200">Matches a valid `double` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1201">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1201">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1202">Coincide con un valor `float` válido (en la referencia cultural invariable; vea la advertencia)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1202">Matches a valid `float` value (in the invariant culture - see warning)</span></span> |
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1203">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1203">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1204">Coincide con un valor `Guid` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1204">Matches a valid `Guid` value</span></span> |
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1205">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1205">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1206">Coincide con un valor `long` válido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1206">Matches a valid `long` value</span></span> |
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1207">La cadena debe tener al menos cuatro caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1207">String must be at least 4 characters</span></span> |
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `Richard` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1208">La cadena no debe tener más de ocho caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1208">String must be no more than 8 characters</span></span> |
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1209">La cadena debe tener una longitud de exactamente 12 caracteres</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1209">String must be exactly 12 characters long</span></span> |
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1210">La cadena debe tener una longitud como mínimo de ocho caracteres y como máximo de 16</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1210">String must be at least 8 and no more than 16 characters long</span></span> |
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1211">El valor entero debe ser como mínimo 18</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1211">Integer value must be at least 18</span></span> |
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1212">El valor entero debe ser como máximo 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1212">Integer value must be no more than 120</span></span> |
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1213">El valor entero debe ser como mínimo 18 y máximo 120</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1213">Integer value must be at least 18 but no more than 120</span></span> |
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1214">La cadena debe constar de uno o más caracteres alfabéticos (`a`-`z`, no distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1214">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters (`a`-`z`, case-insensitive)</span></span> |
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1215">La cadena debe coincidir con la expresión regular (vea las sugerencias sobre cómo definir una expresión regular)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1215">String must match the regular expression (see tips about defining a regular expression)</span></span> |
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1216">Se usa para exigir que un valor que no es de parámetro esté presente durante la generación de dirección URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1216">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1217">Es posible aplicar varias restricciones delimitadas por dos puntos a un único parámetro.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1217">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1218">Por ejemplo, la siguiente restricción permite limitar un parámetro a un valor entero de 1 o superior:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1218">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1219">Las restricciones de ruta que comprueban la dirección URL y que se convierten en un tipo CLR (como `int` o `DateTime`) usan siempre la referencia cultural invariable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1219">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1220">Estas restricciones dan por supuesto que la dirección URL no es localizable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1220">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1221">Las restricciones de ruta proporcionadas por el marco de trabajo no modifican los valores almacenados en los valores de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1221">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1222">Todos los valores de ruta analizados desde la dirección URL se almacenan como cadenas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1222">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1223">Por ejemplo, la restricción `float` intenta convertir el valor de ruta en un valor Float, pero el valor convertido se usa exclusivamente para comprobar que se puede convertir en Float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1223">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1224">Expresiones regulares</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1224">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1225">El marco de trabajo de ASP.NET Core agrega `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` al constructor de expresiones regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1225">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1226">Vea <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> para obtener una descripción de estos miembros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1226">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1227">Las expresiones regulares usan delimitadores y tokens similares a los que usan el enrutamiento y el lenguaje C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1227">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by Routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1228">Es necesario usar secuencias de escape con los tokens de expresiones regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1228">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1229">Para usar la expresión regular `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` en el enrutamiento, los caracteres `\` (una barra diagonal inversa) de la cadena se deben proporcionar como caracteres `\\` (barra diagonal inversa doble) en el archivo de código fuente de C# para que el carácter de escape de cadena `\` tenga una secuencia de escape (a menos que se usen [literales de cadena textuales](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1229">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing, the expression must have the `\` (single backslash) characters provided in the string as `\\` (double backslash) characters in the C# source file in order to escape the `\` string escape character (unless using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1230">Para aplicar secuencias de escape a los caracteres delimitadores de parámetro de enrutamiento (`{`, `}`, `[` y `]`), duplique los caracteres en la expresión (`{{`, `}`, `[[` y `]]`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1230">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters (`{`, `}`, `[`, `]`), double the characters in the expression (`{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1231">En la tabla siguiente se muestra una expresión regular y la versión con la secuencia de escape.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1231">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version.</span></span>
