| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1232">Expresión regular</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1232">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1233">Expresión regular con secuencia de escape</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1233">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1234">Las expresiones regulares que se usan en el enrutamiento suelen empezar con el carácter de acento circunflejo (`^`) y coinciden con la posición inicial de la cadena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1234">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret (`^`) character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1235">Las expresiones suelen terminar con el carácter del signo de dólar (`$`) y coincidir con el final de la cadena.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1235">The expressions often end with the dollar sign (`$`) character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1236">Los caracteres `^` y `$` garantizan que la expresión regular coincide con el valor completo del parámetro de ruta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1236">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1237">Sin los caracteres `^` y `$`, la expresión regular coincide con cualquier subcadena de la cadena, algo que normalmente no es deseable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1237">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1238">En la tabla siguiente se proporcionan ejemplos y se explica por qué coinciden o no.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1238">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1239">Expresión</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1239">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1240">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1240">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1241">Coincidir con</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1241">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1242">Comentario</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1242">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1243">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1243">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1244">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1244">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1245">Coincidencias de subcadenas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1245">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1246">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1246">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1247">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1247">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1248">Coincidencias de subcadenas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1248">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1249">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1249">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1250">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1250">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1251">Coincide con la expresión</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1251">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1252">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1252">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1253">Sí</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1253">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1254">No distingue mayúsculas de minúsculas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1254">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1255">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1255">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1256">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1256">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1257">Vea `^` y `$` más arriba</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1257">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1258">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1258">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1259">No</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1259">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1260">Vea `^` y `$` más arriba</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1260">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1261">Para obtener más información sobre la sintaxis de expresiones regulares, vea [Expresiones regulares de .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1261">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1262">Para restringir un parámetro a un conjunto conocido de valores posibles, use una expresión regular.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1262">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1263">Por ejemplo, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` solo hace coincidir el valor de ruta `action` con `list`, `get` o `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1263">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1264">Si se pasa al diccionario de restricciones, la cadena `^(list|get|create)$` es equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1264">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1265">Las restricciones que se pasan al diccionario de restricciones (no insertado en una plantilla) que no coinciden con una de las restricciones conocidas también se tratan como expresiones regulares.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1265">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1266">Restricciones de ruta personalizadas</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1266">Custom Route Constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1267">Además de las restricciones de ruta integradas, se pueden crear restricciones de ruta personalizadas implementando la interfaz <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1267">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1268">La interfaz <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contiene un único método, `Match`, que devuelve `true` si se cumple la restricción, y `false` en caso contrario.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1268">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1269">Para utilizar una restricción <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personalizada, el tipo de restricción de ruta debe registrarse con el parámetro <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> de la aplicación en el contenedor de servicios de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1269">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1270"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> es un diccionario que asigna claves de restricciones de ruta a implementaciones de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> que validen esas restricciones.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1270">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1271">El parámetro <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> de una aplicación puede actualizarse en `Startup.ConfigureServices` como parte de una llamada a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) o configurando <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directamente con `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1271">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1272">Por ejemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1272">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1273">La restricción puede aplicarse a las rutas de la manera habitual, usando el nombre especificado al registrar el tipo de restricción.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1273">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1274">Por ejemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1274">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1275">Referencia de generación de direcciones URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1275">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1276">En el ejemplo siguiente se muestra cómo se genera un vínculo a una ruta, dado un diccionario de valores de ruta y un valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1276">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1277">El valor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generado al final del ejemplo anterior es `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1277">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1278">El diccionario proporciona los valores de ruta `operation` e `id` de la plantilla "Ruta de paquete de seguimiento", `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1278">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1279">Para obtener más información, vea el código de ejemplo de la sección [Uso de software intermedio de enrutamiento](#use-routing-middleware) o la [aplicación de ejemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1279">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1280">El segundo parámetro del constructor <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> es una colección de *valores de ambiente*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1280">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1281">Los valores de ambiente son adecuados porque limitan el número de valores que el desarrollador debe especificar dentro de un contexto de solicitud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1281">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1282">Los valores de ruta actuales de la solicitud actual se consideran valores de ambiente para la generación de vínculos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1282">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1283">En la acción `About` de `HomeController` de una aplicación ASP.NET Core MVC, no es necesario especificar el valor de ruta de controlador para vincular a la acción `Index` (se usará el valor de ambiente `Home`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1283">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1284">Los valores de ambiente que no coincidan con un parámetro se omiten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1284">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1285">También se omiten los valores de ambiente cuando un valor proporcionado de forma explícita invalida el valor de ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1285">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1286">La coincidencia se produce de izquierda a derecha en la dirección URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1286">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1287">Los valores que se proporcionan de forma explícita pero que no coinciden con un segmento de la ruta se agregan a la cadena de consulta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1287">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1288">En la tabla siguiente se muestra el resultado cuando se usa la plantilla de ruta `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1288">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1289">Valores de ambiente</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1289">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1290">Valores explícitos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1290">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1291">Resultado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1291">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1292">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1292">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1293">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1293">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1294">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1294">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1295">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1295">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1296">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1296">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1297">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1297">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1298">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1298">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1299">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1299">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1300">Si una ruta tiene un valor predeterminado que no se corresponde con un parámetro y ese valor se proporciona de forma explícita, debe coincidir con el valor predeterminado:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1300">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1301">La generación de vínculos solo genera un vínculo para esta ruta si se proporcionan los valores coincidentes para `controller` y `action`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1301">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="52fac-1302">Segmentos complejos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1302">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="52fac-1303">Los segmentos complejos (por ejemplo, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`), se procesan buscando coincidencias de literales de derecha a izquierda de un modo no expansivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1303">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1304">Consulte [este código](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) para obtener una explicación detallada de cómo se comparan los segmentos complejos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1304">See [this code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="52fac-1305">El [código de ejemplo](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) no se usa en ASP.NET Core, pero proporciona una buena explicación de los segmentos complejos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="52fac-1305">The [code sample](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>
